                                                             the

  931 000003D4         Dequeue PROC             {R1-R14}
  932 000003D4         ;*******************************************************
                       ***
  933 000003D4         ;If the queue (whose queue record structure’s address is
                        in R1) is not empty, dequeues
  934 000003D4         ;a character from the queue to R0 and reports success by
                        returning with the C flag
  935 000003D4         ;cleared, (i.e., 0); otherwise only reports failure by r
                       eturning with the C flag set, (i.e., 1).

  937 000003D4         ; Output: R0: Character dequeued
  938 000003D4         ; PSR C flag: Success(0) or Failure (1)
  939 000003D4         ; Modify: R0; APSR
  940 000003D4         ; All other registers remain unchanged on return

                                                            ter than one

                                                            utPointer and
  950 000003E4         ;Store into R0 to be outputed

                                                            ber enueued

  953 000003E8 1C52            ADDS             R2,R2,#1    ; Increment OutPoin

 1141 000004FC         Enqueue PROC             {R0-R14}
 1142 000004FC         ;*******************************************************
                       ***
 1143 000004FC         ;If the queue (whose queue record structure’s address is
                        in R1) is not full, enqueues the
 1144 000004FC         ;character from R0 to the queue and reports success by r
                       eturning with the C flag
 1145 000004FC         ;cleared, (i.e., 0); otherwise only reports failure by r
                       eturning with the C flag set, (i.e., 1).
 1146 000004FC         ; Input: R0: Character to enqueue
 1147 000004FC         ; R1: Address of queue record structure
 1148 000004FC         ; Output: PSR C flag: Success(0) or Failure (1)
 1149 000004FC         ; Modify: APSR
 1150 000004FC         ; All other registers remain unchanged on return
 1151 000004FC         ;*******************************************************
                       ***
 1152 000004FC B47F            PUSH             {R0-R6}
 1153 000004FE         ; R1 is the base value to where 
 1154 000004FE 4A6A            LDR              R2, =Q_BUF_SZ
